google_ad_request_done(google_ads)
{




window['google_ads']
=
google_ads;




if(google_ads.length
!=
0)
{








apply_ad_config(google_ads.length);









render_ads(true,
window['ad_config_top']);









if(window['backfillParam'])
{












window['backfillParam']['pl_rnum']
=
google_ads.length;












window['backfillParam']['pl_time']
=
Date.now()
-
afc_ad_start_time;








}




}
}

function
apply_ad_config(num)
{
window['ad_config_top']
=
Math.min(2,
num);
window['ad_config_bot']
=
Math.min(2,
num);
}

google_ad_client
=
'ca-aj-cat';
google_ad_channel
=
'cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN';
google_ad_output
=
'js';
google_max_num_ads
=
'4';
google_ad_type
=
'text';
google_image_size
=
'';
google_num_ads_recieved=
'';
google_language
=
'';
google_country
=
'';
google_encoding
=
'utf8';
google_safe
=
'medium';
google_adtest
=
'off';
google_ad_section
=
'default';
google_page_url
=
'';
google_hints
=
'Eminem_discography';
google_kw
=
'';
google_kw_type
=
'broad';


var
backfillParam
=
{




pl_rqnum
:
google_max_num_ads,




pl_hints
:
google_hints,




pl_rp
:
"false",




pl_kw
:
google_kw,




pl_cl
:
google_ad_client,




pl_ch
:
google_ad_channel,




pl_hex
:
"#FDFEEE",




pl_type
:
"afc",




pl_clksp
:
"none"};

var
word_arr
;

var
word_arr_len
;


function
highlightQuery(input_str)
{

var
queryTokenArray
=
"eminem,discography,_,";


var
tok_arr
=
queryTokenArray.split(",");

for(tok_arr_idx=0;
tok_arr_idx
<
tok_arr.length-1;
tok_arr_idx
++)
{

if(isCombinationWord(tok_arr[tok_arr_idx])){
word_arr
=
tok_arr[tok_arr_idx].split("-");
word_arr_len
=
word_arr.length;
first_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(word_arr[0],0);

if(first_pos
!=-1)
{
input_str
=
highlightCombinationWords(input_str,first_pos);
}
}
else
{
first_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(tok_arr[tok_arr_idx],0);
if(first_pos
!=
-1
&&
tok_arr[tok_arr_idx].length
>
0)
{
input_str
=
highlightSimpleWords(input_str,tok_arr[tok_arr_idx],first_pos);
}
}
}
return
input_str;
}

function
isCombinationWord(word){
if(word.indexOf("-")
!=
-1){
return
true;
}
else
{
return
false;
}
}


function
isAlpha(ch)
{
if
(ch
!=
null
&&
ch.match(/^[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/)){
return
true;
}
return
false;
}

function
isQueryinInput(firstindex,
input_str,
j){
for(i=firstindex;
i<
input_str.length
;
++i)
{
var
currindex
=
i;

if(!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(i)))
{
if(firstindex
==
currindex)

{
firstindex++;
}
else
{
if(word_arr[j]
!=
input_str.substring(firstindex,currindex).toLowerCase())
return
-1;
if
(j
==
word_arr_len-1)
return
currindex;
else
return
isQueryinInput(currindex+1,input_str,++j);
}
}
}

if(j
<
word_arr_len)
{
if(word_arr[j]
!=
input_str.substring(firstindex,currindex+1).toLowerCase())
return
-1;
}

return
(currindex
+
1)
;
}


function

highlightCombinationWords(input_str,first_pos)
{
exactmatch
=
isQueryinInput(first_pos+word_arr[0].length,input_str,1)
;
if(exactmatch
!=-1
)

{
bold_str
=
"<b>"
+
input_str.substring(first_pos,exactmatch)
+
"</b>";
input_str
=
input_str.substring(0,first_pos)
+
bold_str
+
input_str.substring(exactmatch);
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(word_arr[0],exactmatch+7);
while(next_pos
!=
-1)
{
return
highlightCombinationWords(input_str,next_pos);
}
}
return
input_str;
}


function

highlightSimpleWords(input_str,token,
first_pos)
{
var
end_pos
=
first_pos
+
token.length;
if(!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(end_pos))
&&
!isAlpha(input_str.charAt(first_pos-1))){
bold_str
=
"<b>"
+
input_str.substring(first_pos,end_pos)
+
"</b>";
input_str
=
input_str.substring(0,first_pos)
+
bold_str
+
input_str.substring(end_pos);
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(token,end_pos+7);
}
else
{
next_pos
=
input_str.toLowerCase().indexOf(token,end_pos);
}

while(next_pos
!=
-1)
{
return
highlightSimpleWords(input_str,token,next_pos);
}
return
input_str;
}</script>

<p>The
discography
of
American
rapper
<a
href="/wiki/Eminem?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Eminem">Eminem</a>
includes
eight
released
<a
href="/wiki/Studio_album?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Studio
album"
class="mw-redirect">studio
albums</a>,
four
<a
href="/wiki/Compilation_album?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Compilation
album">compilations</a>,
two
<a
href="/wiki/Extended_plays?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Extended
plays"
class="mw-redirect">extended
plays</a>,
thirty-one
<a
href="/wiki/Single_(music)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Single
(music)">singles</a>,
five
video
albums
and
one
<a
href="/wiki/Soundtrack?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Soundtrack">soundtrack</a>.
His
music
has
been
released
on
record
labels
<a
href="/wiki/Web_Entertainment?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Web
Entertainment">Web
Entertainment</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Interscope_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Interscope
Records">Interscope
Records</a>,
along
with
subsidiaries
<a
href="/wiki/Aftermath_Entertainment?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aftermath
Entertainment">Aftermath
Entertainment</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Goliath_Artists?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Goliath
Artists"
class="mw-redirect">Goliath
Artists</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Shady_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Shady
Records">Shady
Records</a>.
Eminem
is
the
best-selling
hip-hop
artist
of
all-time<sup
id="cite_ref-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
the
best-selling
artist
of
the
2000s<sup
id="cite_ref-UMG_2-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-UMG-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup>
with
US
album
sales
at
over
32.2
million
during
the
decade.<sup
id="cite_ref-decadeartist_3-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-decadeartist-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
total
Eminem
has
sold
43
million
albums
in
the
United
States
as
a
solo
artist.<sup
id="cite_ref-4"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup>
His
worldwide
albums
sales
stand
at
more
than
100
million.<sup
id="cite_ref-5"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
has
earned
forty-two
platinum
certifications
from
the
<a
href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Recording
Industry
Association
of
America">Recording
Industry
Association
of
America</a>
(RIAA).<sup
class="reference"
id="ref_note_a1"><a
href="#endnote_note_a1">[A]</a></sup>
In
this
<a
href="/wiki/Discography?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Discography">discography</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Music_video?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Music
video">music
videos</a>
and
collaborations
are
included
as
well.</p>








<p>In
1996,
Eminem
released
his
first
studio
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Infinite_(Eminem_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Infinite
(Eminem
album)">Infinite</a></i>,
under
Web
Entertainment.
The
album
sold
about
a
thousand
copies<sup
id="cite_ref-infinite_6-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-infinite-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
failed
to
rank
on
the
national
charts.
After
signing
a
contract
with
Interscope
Records
and
Aftermath
Entertainment,
the
rapper
released
his
sophomore
and
commercial
debut
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Slim_Shady_LP?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Slim
Shady
LP">The
Slim
Shady
LP</a></i>
in
1999
and
reached
the
number
two
spot
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_200?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
200"><i>Billboard</i>
200</a>,
and
received
four
platinum
certifications
in
the
United
States
from
the
RIAA.
In
the
same
year,
the
rapper,
along
with
manager
<a
href="/wiki/Paul_Rosenberg_(music_manager)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paul
Rosenberg
(music
manager)">Paul
Rosenberg</a>,
founded
the
<a
href="/wiki/Vanity_label?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Vanity
label">imprint
label</a>
Shady
Records.<sup
id="cite_ref-7"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-8"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
the
subsequent
year,
Eminem
released
his
third
studio
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Marshall_Mathers_LP?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Marshall
Mathers
LP">The
Marshall
Mathers
LP</a></i>,
which
sold
1.76
million
copies
in
its
first
week
of
distribution,
breaking
records
for
the
fastest-selling
hip
hop
album
of
all-time
and
the
fastest-selling
solo
album
in
the
United
States.<sup
id="cite_ref-9"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-10"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup>
With
more
than
ten
million
copies
sold,<sup
id="cite_ref-mmlp_11-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-mmlp-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup>
the
album
was
the
third
best-selling
record
of
the
year
in
the
United
States,<sup
id="cite_ref-12"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup>
where
it
also
earned
nine
platinum
certifications.
The
<a
href="/wiki/Lead_single?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lead
single">lead
single</a>
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/The_Real_Slim_Shady?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Real
Slim
Shady">The
Real
Slim
Shady</a>&quot;
became
Eminem's
first
song
to
enter
in
the
top
ten
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
Hot
100"><i>Billboard</i>
Hot
100</a>.
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Stan_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stan
(song)">Stan</a>&quot;
was
the
most
successful
single
outside
of
the
States,
while
it
failed
to

in

<p>In
2002,
Eminem's
fourth
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Eminem_Show?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Eminem
Show">The
Eminem
Show</a></i>,
debuted
at
number
one
on
the
<i>Billboard</i>
200
and
reached
the
top
spot
on
various
charts
internationally,
as
it
went
on
to
sell
over
nineteen
million
copies
worldwide.<sup
id="cite_ref-TESsold_13-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-TESsold-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
the
United
States,
<i>The
Eminem
Show</i>
was
the
highest-selling
album
of
the
year,<sup
id="cite_ref-14"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-14"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup>
with
sales
of
almost
ten
million
copies.<sup
id="cite_ref-USsales_15-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-USsales-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
album
received
a
diamond
certification
from
the
RIAA
in
2011.
The
album
also
received
a
diamond
certification
in
Canada,
equivalent
to
the
shipment
of
one
million
units.
The
album
received
eight
platinum
certifications
from
New
Zealand's
<a
href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_New_Zealand?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Recording
Industry
Association
of
New
Zealand"
class="mw-redirect">Recording
Industry
Association
of
New
Zealand</a>.
In
the
same
year,
Eminem's
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Lose_Yourself?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lose
Yourself">Lose
Yourself</a>&quot;,
from
the
<a
href="/wiki/8_Mile_(soundtrack)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="8
Mile
(soundtrack)"
class="mw-redirect"><i>8
Mile</i>
soundtrack</a>,
became
the
rapper's
first
number
one
song
on
the
Hot
100
and
remained
on
the
top
for
twelve
weeks.<sup
id="cite_ref-16"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
song
also
reached
the
top
of
various
national
charts
worldwide.
The
<i>8
Mile</i>
soundtrack
peaked
to
the
number
one
position
in
the
United
States,
where
it
sold
more
than
four
million<sup
id="cite_ref-USsales_15-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-USsales-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup>
of
the
nine
million
copies
distributed
internationally.<sup
id="cite_ref-8mileWW_17-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-8mileWW-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
2004,
Eminem's
fifth
studio
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Encore_(Eminem_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Encore
(Eminem
album)">Encore</a></i>
became
the
rapper's
third
consecutive
studio
album
to
reach
number
one
in
the
United
States,
Australia,
Canada,
New
Zealand
and
United
Kingdom.
Sales,
however,
were
significantly
less
than
the
two
previous
studio
albums,
with
over
five
million
sold
copies
in
the
United
States<sup
id="cite_ref-ccth_18-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-ccth-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
eleven
million
worldwide.<sup
id="cite_ref-independent_19-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-independent-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup>
Much
success
for
<i>Encore'</i>s
singles
came
from
the
United
Kingdom,
where
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Just_Lose_It?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Just
Lose
It">Just
Lose
It</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Like_Toy_Soldiers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Like
Toy
Soldiers">Like
Toy
Soldiers</a>&quot;
went
on
to
top
the
<a
href="/wiki/UK_Singles_Chart?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="UK
Singles
Chart">UK
Singles
Chart</a>
and
two
other
songs,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Mockingbird_(Eminem_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mockingbird
(Eminem
song)">Mockingbird</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Ass_Like_That?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ass
Like
That">Ass
Like
That</a>&quot;
reached
position
number
four.
Eminem
released
in
2005
a
<a
href="/wiki/Greatest_hits?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Greatest
hits"
class="mw-redirect">greatest
hits</a>
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Curtain_Call:_The_Hits?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Curtain
Call:
The
Hits">Curtain
Call:
The
Hits</a></i>,
which
sold
almost
three
million
copies
in
the
US<sup
id="cite_ref-ccth_18-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-ccth-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
received
a
double
platinum
certification
from
RIAA.
In
the
following
year,
Shady
Records
released
<i><a
href="/wiki/Eminem_Presents:_The_Re-Up?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Eminem
Presents:
The
Re-Up">Eminem
Presents:
The
Re-Up</a></i>,
a
<a
href="/wiki/Compilation_album?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Compilation
album">compilation
album</a>
performed
by
Eminem
along
various
artists
from
the
record
label.
The
album
received
a
platinum
certification
from
the
RIAA
in
2007
and
sold
slightly
over
a
million
copies
in
the
United
States.<sup
id="cite_ref-USsales_15-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-USsales-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
2009,
the
song
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Crack_a_Bottle?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Crack
a
Bottle">Crack
a
Bottle</a>&quot;,
a
collaboration
with
label-mates
<a
href="/wiki/Dr._Dre?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dr.
Dre">Dr.
Dre</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/50_Cent?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="50
Cent">50
Cent</a>,
became
Eminem's
second
number
one
on
the
Hot
100
and
broke
the
record
for
opening
week
download
sales
in
the
United
States,
with
418,000
copies
sold
in
the
first
week.<sup
id="cite_ref-record_20-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-record-20"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup>
After
a
break
of
more
than
four
years,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Relapse_(Eminem_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Relapse
(Eminem
album)">Relapse</a></i>,
Eminem's
sixth
studio
album,
was
released
in
2009
and
was
the
rapper's
fourth
consecutive
studio
album
to
once
again
top
the
Australia,
Canada,
New
Zealand,
United
Kingdom
and
US
as
well
as
various
worldwide
charts,
with
domestic
sales
of
over
two
million
copies.<sup
id="cite_ref-DX-week-ending-9-12-2010_21-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-DX-week-ending-9-12-2010-21"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
the
subsequent
year,
Eminem
released
his
seventh
studio
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Recovery_(Eminem_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Recovery
(Eminem
album)">Recovery</a></i>,
which
debuted
at
number
one
on
the
<i>Billboard</i>
200
and
reached
the
top
spot
on
various
charts
internationally.
<i>Recovery'</i>s
singles
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Not_Afraid?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Not
Afraid">Not
Afraid</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Love_the_Way_You_Lie?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Love
the
Way
You
Lie">Love
the
Way
You
Lie</a>&quot;
featuring
<a
href="/wiki/Rihanna?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rihanna">Rihanna</a>,
became
the
rapper's
third
and
fourth
number
one
songs
on
the
Hot
100;
the
latter
also
reached
the
top
of
various
national
charts
worldwide.
On
August
25,
2013,
he
released
the
single
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Berzerk_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Berzerk
(song)">Berzerk</a>&quot;
which
debut
at
number
3
on
the
Billboard
Hot
100
and
announced
his
new
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Marshall_Mathers_LP_2?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Marshall
Mathers
LP
2">The
Marshall
Mathers
LP
2</a></i>
which
was
released
on
November
5,
2013,
the
following
singles
were
&quot;Survival&quot;
which
was
showcased
during
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Call_of_Duty:_Ghosts?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Call
of
Duty:
Ghosts">Call
of
Duty:
Ghosts</a></i>
reveal
trailer,<sup
id="cite_ref-22"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-22"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup>
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Rap_God?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rap
God">Rap
God</a>&quot;
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/The_Monster_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Monster
(song)">The
Monster</a>&quot;
featuring
<a
href="/wiki/Rihanna?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rihanna">Rihanna</a>.
As
of
November
2010
Eminem
had
four
songs
that
have
sold
over
three
million
downloads
in
the
United
States.<sup
id="cite_ref-23"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-23"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup>
Eminem
has
sold
more
than
42
million
track
downloads
in
the
United
States
alone.<sup
id="cite_ref-BW-Nielsen_2011_24-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BW-Nielsen_2011-24"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
January
2011
Eminem
was
identified
as
the
first
artist
in
Nielsen
SoundScan
history
to
have
two
year-end
number-one
albums.
Eminem
was
named
the
best
selling
artist
in
Canada
in
2010
and
2013.<sup
id="cite_ref-25"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-25"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-canada_sales_26-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-canada_sales-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<ul>














<li><b>A</b>
<span
class="citation
wikicite"
id="endnote_note_a1"><b><a
href="#ref_note_a1">^</a></b></span>
The
forty-two
platinum
certifications
by
the
<a
href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Recording
Industry
Association
of
America">Recording
Industry
Association
of
America</a>
include
twenty-nine
platinum
certifications
credited
as
a
solo
artist<sup
id="cite_ref-riaa_42-21"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-riaa-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
eleven
certifications
with
various
artists.<sup
id="cite_ref-8mileriaa_91-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-8mileriaa-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-re-upriaa_104-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-re-upriaa-104"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-smokeriaa_111-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-smokeriaa-111"><span>[</span>111<span>]</span></a></sup></li>














<li><b>B</b>
<span
class="citation
wikicite"
id="endnote_note_b1"><b><a
href="#ref_note_b1">^</a></b></span>
The
reported
chart
positions
are
of
the
latter
release
<i>The
Slim
Shady
LP</i>
(Special
Edition).
The
original
album
release
peaked
up
to
number
forty-six
on
the
Belgian
<a
href="/wiki/Ultratop?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ultratop">Ultratop</a>
and
seventy-seven
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Swiss_Record_Charts?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Swiss
Record
Charts"
class="mw-redirect">Swiss
Record
Charts</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-BELAl_29-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BELAl-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-SWIAl_35-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-SWIAl-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup></li>














<li><b>C</b>
<span
class="citation
wikicite"
id="endnote_note_c1"><b><a
href="#ref_note_c1">^</a></b></span>
For
certifications
of
<i>The
Slim
Shady
LP</i>
and
<i>E</i>,
enter
<b>Eminem</b>
in
the
&quot;artist
name&quot;
field.<sup
id="cite_ref-259"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-259"><span>[</span>259<span>]</span></a></sup></li>














<li><b>D</b>
<span
class="citation
wikicite"
id="endnote_note_d1"><b><a
href="#ref_note_d1">^</a></b></span>
The
reported
peak
chart
positions
are
indicative
of
the
UK
Compilation
Albums
Chart,
as
soundtracks
and
compilation
albums
by
various
artists
are
not
eligible
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/UK_Albums_Chart?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="UK
Albums
Chart">UK
Albums
Chart</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-260"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-261"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-261"><span>[</span>261<span>]</span></a></sup></li>














<li><b>E</b>

Don't

<i>Billboard</i>
Hot
100,

<a

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Eminem_discography&page=1&ac=24&qid=CE4D1AB0EA3A44D9226890245FD0C13A&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>




</div>
